Points\\n\\n## 1. WindowAssigner Abstract Base Class\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class WindowAssigner<T, W extends Window>`\\n\\n**Abstract Methods (Extension Points):**\\n- `public abstract Collection<W> assignWindows(T element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context)` - Assigns zero or more windows to an element based on its timestamp and a context that provides current processing time.\\n- `public abstract Trigger<T, W> getDefaultTrigger()` - Returns the default trigger associated with this assigner. Developers can customize trigger behavior for their windowing strategy.\\n- `public abstract TypeSerializer<W> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig)` - Provides a serializer for the specific window type produced by this assigner.\\n- `public abstract boolean isEventTime()` - Indicates whether windows are based on event time (true) or processing time (false).\\n\\n**Inner Class:** `WindowAssignerContext` with method `getCurrentProcessingTime()` for querying current system time.\\n\\n## 2. MergingWindowAssigner Subclass\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class MergingWindowAssigner<T, W extends Window> extends WindowAssigner<T, W>`\\n\\n**Extension Point for Merging:**\\n- `public abstract void mergeWindows(Collection<W> windows, MergeCallback<W> callback)` - Determines which windows should be merged. This is the critical extension point for session-style windows where overlapping or adjacent windows must be combined.\\n\\n**Callback Interface:** `MergeCallback<W>` with method `void merge(Collection<W> toBeMerged, W mergeResult)` for specifying merge results.\\n\\n## 3. Trigger Base Class (Lifecycle Methods)\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class Trigger<T, W extends Window>`\\n\\n**Lifecycle Methods (Extension Points):**\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onElement(T element, long timestamp, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when an element arrives in a window pane. Determines whether the pane should be evaluated.\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when a processing-time timer fires. Allows triggers based on wall-clock time.\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when an event-time timer fires based on watermarks. Enables event-driven triggering.\\n- `public abstract void clear(W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Clears trigger state when a window is purged, including timers.\\n\\n**Merge Support Methods:**\\n- `public boolean canMerge()` - Returns true if the trigger supports window merging (default: false). Must be true for use with MergingWindowAssigner.\\n- `public void onMerge(W window, OnMergeContext ctx)` - Called when windows are merged. Implementations must properly handle trigger state merging.\\n\\n**Context Interfaces:**\\n- `TriggerContext` - Provides access to timer registration, watermarks, metrics, and per-window state.\\n- `OnMergeContext extends TriggerContext` - Extended context for merge operations, with `mergePartitionedState()` method.\\n\\n## 4. Reference Implementation: EventTimeSessionWindows\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public class EventTimeSessionWindows extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>`\\n\\n**Implementation Pattern:**\\n\\n**assignWindows() Implementation:**\\n```java\\npublic Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\\n    return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(timestamp, timestamp + sessionTimeout));\\n}\\n```\\nCreates a single TimeWindow starting at the element's timestamp and extending by the session gap/timeout.\\n\\n**mergeWindows() Implementation:**\\n```java\\npublic void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\\n    TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\\n}\\n```\\nDelegates to the static `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` method which handles overlap detection and merging of overlapping session windows.\\n\\n**Other Methods:**\\n- `getDefaultTrigger()` returns `EventTimeTrigger.create()` - Triggers are fired based on event time progress (watermarks).\\n- `isEventTime()` returns true - Session windows are based on element timestamps, not processing time.\\n- `getWindowSerializer()` returns `new TimeWindow.Serializer()` - Uses TimeWindow's standard serialization.\\n\\n## 5. TimeWindow Class (Window Type)\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public class TimeWindow extends Window`\\n\\n**Fields:**\\n- `private final long start` - Window start time (inclusive).\\n- `private final long end` - Window end time (exclusive).\\n\\n**Constructor:**\\n- `public TimeWindow(long start, long end)` - Creates a time window for the given timestamp range.\\n\\n**Key Methods:**\\n- `public static void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c)` - Static utility method used by session window assigners to merge overlapping TimeWindows. This is the core merging logic: windows are sorted, and overlapping windows are identified and merged into larger windows.\\n- `public TimeWindow cover(TimeWindow other)` - Returns the minimal window covering both this and another window, used internally for merge results.\\n\\n**Inner Class:**\\n- `public static class Serializer extends TypeSerializerSingleton<TimeWindow>` - Handles serialization/deserialization of TimeWindow objects for checkpointing and state backend storage.\\n\\n## Extension Point Summary\\nA developer implementing a custom window assigner must:\\n1. Extend `WindowAssigner` and implement `assignWindows()`, `getDefaultTrigger()`, `getWindowSerializer()`, and `isEventTime()`.\\n2. For merging windows (like sessions), extend `MergingWindowAssigner` and implement `mergeWindows()`.\\n3. Points\\n\\n## 1. WindowAssigner Abstract Base Class\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class WindowAssigner<T, W extends Window>`\\n\\n**Abstract Methods (Extension Points):**\\n- `public abstract Collection<W> assignWindows(T element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context)` - Assigns zero or more windows to an element based on its timestamp and a context that provides current processing time.\\n- `public abstract Trigger<T, W> getDefaultTrigger()` - Returns the default trigger associated with this assigner. Developers can customize trigger behavior for their windowing strategy.\\n- `public abstract TypeSerializer<W> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig)` - Provides a serializer for the specific window type produced by this assigner.\\n- `public abstract boolean isEventTime()` - Indicates whether windows are based on event time (true) or processing time (false).\\n\\n**Inner Class:** `WindowAssignerContext` with method `getCurrentProcessingTime()` for querying current system time.\\n\\n## 2. MergingWindowAssigner Subclass\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class MergingWindowAssigner<T, W extends Window> extends WindowAssigner<T, W>`\\n\\n**Extension Point for Merging:**\\n- `public abstract void mergeWindows(Collection<W> windows, MergeCallback<W> callback)` - Determines which windows should be merged. This is the critical extension point for session-style windows where overlapping or adjacent windows must be combined.\\n\\n**Callback Interface:** `MergeCallback<W>` with method `void merge(Collection<W> toBeMerged, W mergeResult)` for specifying merge results.\\n\\n## 3. Trigger Base Class (Lifecycle Methods)\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class Trigger<T, W extends Window>`\\n\\n**Lifecycle Methods (Extension Points):**\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onElement(T element, long timestamp, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when an element arrives in a window pane. Determines whether the pane should be evaluated.\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when a processing-time timer fires. Allows triggers based on wall-clock time.\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Called when an event-time timer fires based on watermarks. Enables event-driven triggering.\\n- `public abstract void clear(W window, TriggerContext ctx)` - Clears trigger state when a window is purged, including timers.\\n\\n**Merge Support Methods:**\\n- `public boolean canMerge()` - Returns true if the trigger supports window merging (default: false). Must be true for use with MergingWindowAssigner.\\n- `public void onMerge(W window, OnMergeContext ctx)` - Called when windows are merged. Implementations must properly handle trigger state merging.\\n\\n**Context Interfaces:**\\n- `TriggerContext` - Provides access to timer registration, watermarks, metrics, and per-window state.\\n- `OnMergeContext extends TriggerContext` - Extended context for merge operations, with `mergePartitionedState()` method.\\n\\n## 4. Reference Implementation: EventTimeSessionWindows\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public class EventTimeSessionWindows extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>`\\n\\n**Implementation Pattern:**\\n\\n**assignWindows() Implementation:**\\n```java\\npublic Collection<TimeWindow> assignWindows(Object element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context) {\\n    return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(timestamp, timestamp + sessionTimeout));\\n}\\n```\\nCreates a single TimeWindow starting at the element's timestamp and extending by the session gap/timeout.\\n\\n**mergeWindows() Implementation:**\\n```java\\npublic void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c) {\\n    TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);\\n}\\n```\\nDelegates to the static `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` method which handles overlap detection and merging of overlapping session windows.\\n\\n**Other Methods:**\\n- `getDefaultTrigger()` returns `EventTimeTrigger.create()` - Triggers are fired based on event time progress (watermarks).\\n- `isEventTime()` returns true - Session windows are based on element timestamps, not processing time.\\n- `getWindowSerializer()` returns `new TimeWindow.Serializer()` - Uses TimeWindow's standard serialization.\\n\\n## 5. TimeWindow Class (Window Type)\\n**Location:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java`\\n\\n**Class:** `public class TimeWindow extends Window`\\n\\n**Fields:**\\n- `private final long start` - Window start time (inclusive).\\n- `private final long end` - Window end time (exclusive).\\n\\n**Constructor:**\\n- `public TimeWindow(long start, long end)` - Creates a time window for the given timestamp range.\\n\\n**Key Methods:**\\n- `public static void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c)` - Static utility method used by session window assigners to merge overlapping TimeWindows. This is the core merging logic: windows are sorted, and overlapping windows are identified and merged into larger windows.\\n- `public TimeWindow cover(TimeWindow other)` - Returns the minimal window covering both this and another window, used internally for merge results.\\n\\n**Inner Class:**\\n- `public static class Serializer extends TypeSerializerSingleton<TimeWindow>` - Handles serialization/deserialization of TimeWindow objects for checkpointing and state backend storage.\\n\\n## Extension Point Summary\\nA developer implementing a custom window assigner must:\\n1. Extend `WindowAssigner` and implement `assignWindows()`, `getDefaultTrigger()`, `getWindowSerializer()`, and `isEventTime()`.\\n2. For merging windows (like sessions), extend `MergingWindowAssigner` and implement `mergeWindows()`.\\n3. Optionally implement a custom `Trigger` by extending `Trigger` and implementing all lifecycle methods: `onElement()`, `onProcessingTime()`, `onEventTime()`, and `clear()`. If using with a `MergingWindowAssigner`, also override `canMerge()` to return true and implement `onMerge()`.\\n4. Choose or create a `Window` subclass (e.g., `TimeWindow`) to represent the window boundaries.\\n\\nThe EventTimeSessionWindows demonstrates this pattern: it assigns each element to a session window of the configured timeout duration, delegates merging to TimeWindow's utility method, and uses EventTimeTrigger for event-driven firing.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
